We would like to address this topic in the most understandable language here.\r\n\r\nWe do NOT collect anonymous usage data using an industry standard third party analytics (Google Analytics) while using the extension.\r\n\r\nWe only store the saved settings for each visited website of each Night Eye user in their localStorage (your computer).
